\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\begin{DoxyVerb}Handle storing and drawing of text in window or data coordinates.\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source_l00095}{95}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source}{text.\+py}}.



\doxysubsection{Constructor \& Destructor Documentation}
\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a2029e12c87c56e99b6bcdaf266582992}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!\_\_init\_\_@{\_\_init\_\_}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_\_init\_\_()}{\_\_init\_\_()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a2029e12c87c56e99b6bcdaf266582992} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+\_\+\+\_\+init\+\_\+\+\_\+ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{x}{ = {\ttfamily 0}, }\item[{}]{y}{ = {\ttfamily 0}, }\item[{}]{text}{ = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}}, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{}]{color}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{}]{verticalalignment}{ = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}baseline\textquotesingle{}}, }\item[{}]{horizontalalignment}{ = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}left\textquotesingle{}}, }\item[{}]{multialignment}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{}]{fontproperties}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{}]{rotation}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{}]{linespacing}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{}]{rotation\+\_\+mode}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{}]{usetex}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{}]{wrap}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{}]{transform\+\_\+rotates\+\_\+text}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{}]{parse\+\_\+math}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{}]{antialiased}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{kwargs}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Create a `.Text` instance at *x*, *y* with string *text*.

The text is aligned relative to the anchor point (*x*, *y*) according
to ``horizontalalignment`` (default: 'left') and ``verticalalignment``
(default: 'baseline'). See also
:doc:`/gallery/text_labels_and_annotations/text_alignment`.

While Text accepts the 'label' keyword argument, by default it is not
added to the handles of a legend.

Valid keyword arguments are:

%(Text:kwdoc)s
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source_l00104}{104}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source}{text.\+py}}.

\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a8a69ac19859e0047e7c120103d9bd449}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!\_char\_index\_at@{\_char\_index\_at}}
\index{\_char\_index\_at@{\_char\_index\_at}!matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_char\_index\_at()}{\_char\_index\_at()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a8a69ac19859e0047e7c120103d9bd449} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+\_\+char\+\_\+index\+\_\+at (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Calculate the index closest to the coordinate x in display space.

The position of text[index] is assumed to be the sum of the widths
of all preceding characters text[:index].

This works only on single line texts.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source_l00252}{252}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source}{text.\+py}}.

\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_ad19eab07399c7295de264523babb8b4e}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!\_preprocess\_math@{\_preprocess\_math}}
\index{\_preprocess\_math@{\_preprocess\_math}!matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_preprocess\_math()}{\_preprocess\_math()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_ad19eab07399c7295de264523babb8b4e} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+\_\+preprocess\+\_\+math (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{s}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Return the string *s* after mathtext preprocessing, and the kind of
mathtext support needed.

- If *self* is configured to use TeX, return *s* unchanged except that
  a single space gets escaped, and the flag "TeX".
- Otherwise, if *s* is mathtext (has an even number of unescaped dollar
  signs) and ``parse_math`` is not set to False, return *s* and the
  flag True.
- Otherwise, return *s* with dollar signs unescaped, and the flag
  False.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a6dcff7c09a580789b263a05b069595d6}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!get\_window\_extent@{get\_window\_extent}}
\index{get\_window\_extent@{get\_window\_extent}!matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_window\_extent()}{get\_window\_extent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a6dcff7c09a580789b263a05b069595d6} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+get\+\_\+window\+\_\+extent (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{renderer}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{}]{dpi}{ = {\ttfamily None}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Return the `.Bbox` bounding the text, in display units.

In addition to being used internally, this is useful for specifying
clickable regions in a png file on a web page.

Parameters
----------
renderer : Renderer, optional
    A renderer is needed to compute the bounding box.  If the artist
    has already been drawn, the renderer is cached; thus, it is only
    necessary to pass this argument when calling `get_window_extent`
    before the first draw.  In practice, it is usually easier to
    trigger a draw first, e.g. by calling
    `~.Figure.draw_without_rendering` or ``plt.show()``.

dpi : float, optional
    The dpi value for computing the bbox, defaults to
    ``self.get_figure(root=True).dpi`` (*not* the renderer dpi); should be set
    e.g. if to match regions with a figure saved with a custom dpi value.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Annotation_a37b7fc7be848a02c6ec072157f1e3afd}{matplotlib.\+text.\+Annotation}}.



Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source_l00926}{926}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source}{text.\+py}}.

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set whether to use antialiased rendering.

Parameters
----------
antialiased : bool

Notes
-----
Antialiasing will be determined by :rc:`text.antialiased`
and the parameter *antialiased* will have no effect if the text contains
math expressions.
\end{DoxyVerb}

Parameters
----------

     scale of the `.patches.FancyBboxPatch` is set to the fontsize.

::

    t.set_bbox(dict(facecolor='red', alpha=0.5))

\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_aa5ed506beafe883ce2b7e70eac5d013d}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!set\_fontfamily@{set\_fontfamily}}
\index{set\_fontfamily@{set\_fontfamily}!matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_fontfamily()}{set\_fontfamily()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_aa5ed506beafe883ce2b7e70eac5d013d} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+set\+\_\+fontfamily (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{fontname}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set the font family.  Can be either a single string, or a list of
strings in decreasing priority.  Each string may be either a real font
name or a generic font class name.  If the latter, the specific font
names will be looked up in the corresponding rcParams.

If a `Text` instance is constructed with ``fontfamily=None``, then the
font is set to :rc:`font.family`, and the
same is done when `set_fontfamily()` is called on an existing
`Text` instance.

Parameters
----------
fontname : {FONTNAME, 'serif', 'sans-serif', 'cursive', 'fantasy', \
'monospace'}

See Also
--------
.font_manager.FontProperties.set_family
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source_l01054}{1054}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source}{text.\+py}}.

\begin{DoxyVerb}Alias for `set_fontfamily`.

----------

'monospace'}

\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_aa98ff06b03c2037643dc71607817255e}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!set\_fontproperties@{set\_fontproperties}}
\index{set\_fontproperties@{set\_fontproperties}!matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_fontproperties()}{set\_fontproperties()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_aa98ff06b03c2037643dc71607817255e} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+set\+\_\+fontproperties (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{fp}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set the font properties that control the text.

Parameters
----------
fp : `.font_manager.FontProperties` or `str` or `pathlib.Path`
    If a `str`, it is interpreted as a fontconfig pattern parsed by
    `.FontProperties`.  If a `pathlib.Path`, it is interpreted as the
    absolute path to a font file.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a78e56d425aa136cd2d6883dc290e0782}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!set\_math\_fontfamily@{set\_math\_fontfamily}}
\index{set\_math\_fontfamily@{set\_math\_fontfamily}!matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_math\_fontfamily()}{set\_math\_fontfamily()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a78e56d425aa136cd2d6883dc290e0782} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+set\+\_\+math\+\_\+fontfamily (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{fontfamily}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set the font family for math text rendered by Matplotlib.

This does only affect Matplotlib's own math renderer. It has no effect
when rendering with TeX (``usetex=True``).

Parameters
----------
fontfamily : str
    The name of the font family.

    Available font families are defined in the
    :ref:`default matplotlibrc file
    <customizing-with-matplotlibrc-files>`.

See Also
--------
get_math_fontfamily
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source_l01138}{1138}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source}{text.\+py}}.

matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+set\+\_\+multialignment (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{align}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set the text alignment for multiline texts.

The layout of the bounding box of all the lines is determined by the
horizontalalignment and verticalalignment properties. This property
controls the alignment of the text lines within that box.

Parameters
----------
align : {'left', 'right', 'center'}
\end{DoxyVerb}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_parse\_math()}{set\_parse\_math()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a5cf3598cfc1f0e9d75fc92e9ec090a2e} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+set\+\_\+parse\+\_\+math (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{parse\+\_\+math}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Override switch to disable any mathtext parsing for this `Text`.

Parameters
----------
parse_math : bool
    If False, this `Text` will never use mathtext.  If True, mathtext
    will be used if there is an even number of unescaped dollar signs.
\end{DoxyVerb}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_af8169ac55774e551a803fc20be68a188} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+set\+\_\+rotation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{s}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set the rotation of the text.

Parameters
----------
s : float or {'vertical', 'horizontal'}
    The rotation angle in degrees in mathematically positive direction
    (counterclockwise). 'horizontal' equals 0, 'vertical' equals 90.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_ae9b15dd6765fe9e7d8c094df3c725d47}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!set\_rotation\_mode@{set\_rotation\_mode}}
\index{set\_rotation\_mode@{set\_rotation\_mode}!matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_rotation\_mode()}{set\_rotation\_mode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_ae9b15dd6765fe9e7d8c094df3c725d47} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+set\+\_\+rotation\+\_\+mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{m}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set text rotation mode.

Parameters
----------
m : {None, 'default', 'anchor'}
    If ``"default"``, the text will be first rotated, then aligned according
    to their horizontal and vertical alignments.  If ``"anchor"``, then
    alignment occurs before rotation. Passing ``None`` will set the rotation
    mode to ``"default"``.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source_l00298}{298}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source}{text.\+py}}.

\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a2156914ba9027a0b840bf41e896b182b}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!set\_text@{set\_text}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_text()}{set\_text()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a2156914ba9027a0b840bf41e896b182b} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+set\+\_\+text (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{s}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set the text string *s*.

It may contain newlines (``\n``) or math in LaTeX syntax.

Parameters
----------
s : object
Any object gets converted to its `str` representation, except for
``None`` which is converted to an empty string.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a9a11f4a61d2668667f59ab29568c08c8}\index{matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}!set\_wrap@{set\_wrap}}
\index{set\_wrap@{set\_wrap}!matplotlib.text.Text@{matplotlib.text.Text}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_wrap()}{set\_wrap()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classmatplotlib_1_1text_1_1Text_a9a11f4a61d2668667f59ab29568c08c8} 
matplotlib.\+text.\+Text.\+set\+\_\+wrap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{wrap}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Set whether the text can be wrapped.

Wrapping makes sure the text is confined to the (sub)figure box. It
does not take into account any other artists.

Parameters
----------
wrap : bool

Notes
-----
Wrapping does not work together with
``savefig(..., bbox_inches='tight')`` (which is also used internally
by ``%matplotlib inline`` in IPython/Jupyter). The 'tight' setting
rescales the canvas to accommodate all content and happens before
wrapping.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source_l00606}{606}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{matplotlib_2text_8py_source}{text.\+py}}.

\begin{DoxyVerb}Update the location and the size of the bbox.

This method should be used when the position and size of the bbox needs
to be updated before actually drawing the bbox.
\end{DoxyVerb}
